## ℹ️ How to Read This Report

| Symbol | Meaning |
|--------|---------|
| ▲ **+N** | Elo gained from this fight |
| ▼ −N | Elo lost from this fight |
| ✅ W | Win |
| ❌ L | Loss |
| ➖ D | Draw or No Contest |
| Before / After | Elo entering and leaving the fight |
| vs Peak | How far current Elo is from their career high |

> **Note:** *Before* reflects post-inactivity-decay elo. Gaps between fights where a fighter lost elo to inactivity will appear as a lower *Before* than the previous *After*.
